kuphela uma iyophuza. Ize iwashiye sekusele usuku olulodwa aehanyuselwe asale aehamusele ingasekho amaehwane azibonele njengawazo zonke izinyoka. 
4.2.7.4 Ukudla ekudlayo 
Ithanda ukudla izimbila. Iyawadla namagundane, izinyoni ikakhulukazi izimpangele. Vma isikhule ngokwanele iyazibamba izinyamazane ezinjengamawule, amaqhina, amazinyane, noma izinyamu zezinye izinyamazane eziphakathi nendawo ngobukhulu ezinjengezimpala, amaphiva, onkonka kanye nezezinyamazane ezinkulu ezingangomgankla. Vma isikubambile ebikuhlasela iyakuginga. Vma yesuthi iyazihlala izinyanga ezi-3 kuya kweziyi-6 ingadli. 
Ayibagingi aban!u inhlwathi. Kodwa asikuphiki ukuthi ingayiginga ingane njengoba sizwa ukuthi endulo zazibaginga abafana ekwaluseni. 
4.2.7.5 lmikhuba nokuziphatha kwayo 
Yinyoka eyesatshwa kakhulu lena. Yesatshelwa ukuthi iyaginga. Iyathanda ukuzilalela nje. Inezinzwa olimini Iwayo ezwa ngazo ngisho emnyameni lapho ingakhona inyamazane noma lokho efuna ukukubamba. Iqala ngokuyibamba ngamazinyo maqede bese iyayizongolozela ngokushesha. 
Ngenkathi isilwane esibambile sinyakaza sigxuma sizama ukuzikhulula iyasimpitsha iziqinise size siphelelwe ngumoya sife. Isephula amathambo bese iyasiginga. Vma isiginga iqala ngekhanda. 
Okunye edume ngakho Ie nyoka ukuthi iguquguqula imibala yenzela ukuheha inyamazane noma inyoni isondele kuyo bese iyayidumela. Empeleni ayiyiguquli imibala inhlwathi. Okwenzekayo kodwa ukukhanya kwelanga okuthi uma kuhlaba emibaleni yayo emihle esesiyiehazile, kwedlula ezihlokweni zezihlahla notshani, ikhazimule kube sengathi umbala wayo uyaguquka. Noma singakaze siyelamele ikwenza lokhu ekuhlangabezaneni kwethu okuningi nayo, Ie nyoka ukuthi iyalutha ngamehlo nemibala yayo, siyakwazi. 
4.2.7.6 Okunye okuphathelene nenhlwathi 
Inhlwathi inezinyama eziqine kakhulu. Yizo phela lezi empitsha ngazo inyamazane. Iyazinweba iziqinise njengoba kwenza laba bantu okuthiwa ngosozinyama. Yiso lesi senzo sayo futhi esenza ingafi kalula ngisho inyathelwe isondo lemoto. 
Ayilingani inhlwathi yensikazi neyenduna. Eyenduna ineane. Kodwa

4.3 	Izinyoka ezingamadlozi 
4.3.1 	Isingeniso 
Kukhona izinyoka ezingalokothwa zibulawe ngisho zingangena endlini. Ingani phela nakhu zingamadlozi. Vma kungene enye yazo ekhaya noma endlini kusuke kubuye abalele bakulowo muzi besazolunguza abantababo nempahla yabo ukuthi kusaphila yini. Nazi ezinye zalezo zinyoka: 
4.3.2 
Ifulwa 
4.3.2.1 lsakhiwo salo 
Ziningana izinhlobo zale nyoka kule ngxenye esikuyo ye-Afrika. Zifikile esihlanwini. Kodwa thin a sizoxoxa ngolulodwa okuyilona Iwejwayeleke kakhulu eningini labantu bakithi. 
Lena yinyoka eluhlaza ewe okotshani. Ifana neamashi nemamba eluhlaza. Vngaze udideke uthi yiyona kodwa eseneane. Vmehluko osobala ukuthi ifulwa lona Iinamangqumuza amehlo. Ngobude ingamasentimitha angama-80. 
4.3.2.2 lndawo eliphila kuyo

4.3.2.3 Ukuzalana kwazo

4.3.2.4 Ukudla ekudlayo 
Le nyoka idla amaselesele, izibankwa nezinambuzane. 
4.3.2.5 Ukuziphatha kwayo 
::'j-

phakathi kwamazwane kanti ixoxo lona alivamile ukuba nalolu ntwentwesana. Okokugcina, ixoxo lihlala ngaphandle kwamanzi. Emanzini amaxoxo aya kuphela ngesikhathi sokuzekana nokuzalela, kanti izingxangxa zona ikhaya lazo lisemanzini. 
Ngokobufakazi obuqoshwe phansi ngomunye wabangane bethu osasishiya emhlabeni uDokotela u Vincent Wager nowaewaninga kabanzi ngalezi zilokazana ezinhle kepha zibe zinganakekile, leli lakithi lieebe kakhulu ngamaselesele. Lidume ngayo inkani nje kuphela, kanye nomsindo-ke. Alithandwa. Liyesatshwa. Hleze kube yilokhu kwenyanywa kwalo okubanga kuhanjelwe kude nalo bese lingazizwa njengeningi lezilwane.

.3.1 	Ukuzalana kwawo 
Malungana nokuzalana kwamaselesele kuzokhumbuleka ukuthi ezwakala njalo ukuthwasa kwehlobo eklaklabula eklabalasa ngamaphimbo awo kulezi zindawo esezichazwe ngenhla, ngezikhathi zakusihlwa. Amaselesele ahlabelelayo kusuke kungawezinkunzi asuke ecula nje ngenhloso yokuheha awesifazane. Asuke eshela. Asuke emi osebeni lomfula, lwedamu, njalonjalo. Izinsikazi zona zisuke ziphakathi emanzini. Impumelelo ekwesheleni kulezi zilwane isekuthini inkunzi ikwazi ukuklabalasa kangakanani. Akubona ubumnandi bomculo kodwa ukuphakama kwephimbo noma ngumklabalaso obalulekile. Isifazane siya ngobuningi baso kuleyo nkunzi eklabalasa okwedlula zooke ezinye zohlobo Iwayo. Ithi ingamkhetha emthandayo inkunzi bese ithi khwenxe emhlane isibebile kulowo esimkhethile. Yiwo lawaya eyongena emanzini. 
Emuva kokuzalelwa kwamaqanda yinsikazi umnumzane uyehla emhlane abuyele endaweni yakhe. Lunye uhlobo Iweselesele olungazaleli emanzini. Kodwa lona lizalela phezulu ezihlahleni. Nalo kodwa likhetha izihlahla ezimile phezu kwamanzi ukuze abantwana balo uma sebechanyuselwa baphonseke emanzini. Phela leli selesele eliyingxangxa yileli elimancadasi elinemilenze emide, namehlokazi angamangqumuza, nezihluzukazi. Kokunye libamdaka kanti elinye libaluhlaza bese Iihloba ngombala omdaka noma othuma oyimisho. Mahle la maselesele. Kuthiwa yizingxangxa zasezihlahleni.

6.2.1.3 [zigaba zokukhula kwenyosi 6.2.1.3.1 Indlovukazi 
Kokuthathu indlovukazi, isisebenzi novongwe kudabuka ngokuchanyuselwa eqandeni elizalelwa yindlovukazi cqeni, esidlekeni sazo izinyosi. 
Ake siqale laphaya eqeni eselinamaqanda aseqede izinsuku eziyi-16 azalelwa yindlovukazi endala yawashiya yafuduka (swarming) nezinye zezisebenzi yaya enxiweni elisha cthangeni. 
Amaqanda ukuthi yiliphi elichanyusel wa kuqala nelichanyuselwa muva kuya ngokuthi yiliphi elabekwa kuqala futhi yiliphi elabekwa kamuva. Akukhathaleki ukuthi ashiyana ngesikhathi esingakanani ekubekweni kwawo. Indlovukazi ephuma kuqala eqandeni ngalolu suku, izungeza kulO lOnke izindawo ezinamaqanda azalelwe ezikhaleni zamaqanda achamusela izindlovukazi. Izisebenzi aziyivumeli ukuba ikwenze lokhu. Kungale nkathi-ke lapho ithi ukuzindazindela ize ibonwe ngovongwe bese isuka indize iqonde emkhathini lapho izekelwa khona ngomunye wovongwe.

Kuhle sikuveze lapha ukuthi njengoba imbewu okuyiyona evundisa amaqanda abekwa yindlovukazi esidlekeni sezinyosi ivuthulelwa yiyo indlovukazi, amaqanda okulOchanyuselwa kuwona ovongwe akayitholi won a Ie nhlwanyelo. 6.2. 1.4 Ukwehlukaniswa noma ukwabiwa kwemisebenzi esidlekeni sezinyosi

6.2.1.4.2 Izisebenzi 
Ngasohlangothini Iwempilo yezinyosi izisebenzi yilOna ezibaluleke kakhulu njengoba sizobona nje. 
Ezinsukwini zokuqala ezintathu izisebenzi ziphumile emaqeni (zichanyuselwe) umsebenzi wazo wokuqala ukuhlanza izikhala zamaqe lapho ziphume khona (zichanyuselwe khona, amagobolondo). 
Kusuka ezinsukwini eziyisithupha kuya kweziyi-13 zifunza amaqhimiza achanyuselwe ngemuva kwazo. Kusekupheleni kwaso lesi sikhathi lapho ziqala khona ukufunda ukundiza. 
Kusuka ezinsukwini eziyi- 14 kuya kweziyi-17 ziyaqala ukuhlanza umuzi wazo ngokususa izinyosi ezifile nokubeka impova efika nezinye elhala. Ziwuqala ngaso Iesi sikhathi nomshikashika wokwakha amaqe. 
Kusukeia ezinsukwini eziyi-18 kuya kwezingama-ZO umsebenzi wazo omkhulu ukuqapha isidleke sazo.

6.2.1.7 Ukuxhumana kwezinyosi 
Izinyosi zinendlela yaw eyisimanga yokuxhumana. Okokuqala ezazana ngakho izinyosi zesidleke esisodwa yiphunga lazo clifanayo. Naphakathi kwaw izisebenzi zeWukaniswa ngemisebenzi yazoo Lew okuYlzona ezmgabathungathi bendawo ezoba yikhaya elisha kuthiwa ngamavulandlela kanti lew ezithungatha zihlwaye ukudla kuthiwa ngabahlwayi. Uma indawo ingekude ~unamamitha .ay~-lOO inyosi izobika ngo~,shaya indlamu ijilingane !zungeze okuymdllmga.

6.2.1.4.3 Ovongwe 
Ovongwe nabo njengendlovukazi banomsebenzi owodwa yo. Lowo ukuba oyedwa wabo agcagce nendlovukazi. Njengoba benganaludosi nje abakwazi ukulwa, abakwazi ukwenza namunye nje wemisebenzi ebalwe ngaphansi kwezisebenzi. Into abayaziyo nje yikho ukuhuqa ukudla. Yingakho izisebenzi zibantinyela zibabulale nje uma sekuyisikhathi sendlala. Nabo babaluleke kakhulu ngokuba yizinzalanyosi. 
6.2.1.5 Ukuziphatha kwezinyosi 
Yizinambuzane eziyisimangaliso lezi. Zihlakaniphile, zikhuthele kanti zinolaka futhi. Uhlobo lwezinyosi zakuleli lakithi Iwesatshwa umhlaba wonke. Kukhona amazwe okuyicala kuwo ukungenisa lolu hlobo Iwenyosi. Okunye ezidume ngakho ukushesha kwaw ukuthukuthela, ukuxosha kwazo isitha saw isikhathi eside noma ibanga elide. Ziyakuxosha ibanga elingamamitha ayi-lOO, kusukela esidlekeni saw. Uma zike zachukuluzwa zithukuthela zilwe usuku lonke. 
Njengoba udosi Iwenyosi lunojojwana okuyiva, uma isisintinyela isitha sayo, udosi luyahlephuka luhlibuke nenyama yenyosi, lubambelele enyameni ycsitha. Ngenxa yalokhu kulimala, inyosi ayiphili emuva kokuntinyela. Iyafa emuva kwemizuzwana engcmingaki. Ziyambulala umuntu noma isilwane uma zintinyele zaziningi. Bakhona-ke nabantinyelwa czimbalwa bavuvuke wonke umzimba babe yizingqikili. 
6.2. J .6 Ukuzalana kwazo 
Sesikushilo ukuthi yindlovukazi kuphela ezalelayo esidlekeni sezinyosi. Sikuvezile nokuthi nguvongwe oyedwa ofcza umsebenzi wobudoda. Sithe umgcagco wakonyosi ugcagcela Ie phezulu emkhathini. Uma kusasukwa phansi indlovukazi indiza ngejubane elingakaze libonwe besayilandela bebaningi ovongwe. Abanye

6.2.2.2. Ama/unga omndeni 
Owemihlwa umndeni unala malunga: 
6.2.2.2.\ Indlovukazi (uqumbu) 
Nakhona lapha indlovukazi yiyona mzali wezinhlwa. Uma isikhule ngokwanele yehlukaniseka kalula kwamanye amalunga omndeni. Yona ibonakala ngomzimba wayo ongamapaklaza kwesingenzansi kanye nesifuba nekhanda OkunCanyanyana. 
6.2.2.2.2 Inkosi 
Imihlwa. inenkosi. Lapha akufani nasezinyosini lapho ovongwe kungashlwo khona ukuthi ngamakhosi. Inkosi ayehlukile kangako ezisebenzini. Ithi ayibe ngangazo ngokwesakhiwo somzimba. 
6.2.2.2.3 Izisebenzi

150

[zinambuzane
151 



Umehluko osobala ukuthi isakhiwo somzimba wesisebenzi sehlukile kwesesotsha. Asikulungele ukulwa, kodwa silungele ukusebenza kuphela. Ziyizimpumputhe izisebenzi. 
6.2.2.2.4 Amasotsha 
Amasotsha abonakala ngokuba namakhanda amakhulu amade kanye nezinzavula zamazinyo amabili. Nornzimba wesotsha mude kunowesisebenzi. Sibonile ezinyosini ukuthi izisebenzi yilOna futhi amasotsha. 
6.2.2.3 Ukwakheka kon11ldeni wemihlwa 
Lapha-ke silOqala ezinhlwabusini. Abanye bayehlukanisa phakathi kwezinhlwabusi nezinkulungwane. Bathi izinkulungwane yilezi esizibona zindiza ngobuningi bazo ziphuma esidulini zindize emuva kwezimvula noma ngesikhathi sezimvula entwasahlobo nasehlobo. Zimnyama ngombala bese ziba nemishwana emincanyanyana emhloshana ezungeza kwesingenzansi. 
Labo.ke bathi uma izinkulungwane sezehlele phansi emhlabathini zakuyeka ukundiza zawohloka nezimpiko kuba yizinhlwabusi. Zibabomvu ngokunsundu ngombala. Ibakhona imisho nalapha, kodwa yona ibathuma ngombala. Thina-ke lapha asizokwehlukanisa ngoba lokhu kwehlukana kungokwamazinga okukhula nje kuphela. Ngakho-ke sizosebenzisa igama elithi izinhlwabusi ukuchaza lokhu kokubili. 
Sonke sike sizibone izinhlwabusi zindiza sekungathi amafu emkhathini, ziphuma esidulini. Kusuke kuyizindlovukazi, oqumbu phela kanye nabakhwenyana babo amakhosi angomuso. Nakhona lapha uqumbu nenkosi akungaze kungashiwo ukuthi sekunguqumbu nokuthi yinkosi uma kungakazinzi esigodlweni sakho esidulini okuyinganga. Konke kuba yizinhlwabusi. Lezi zinhlwabusi zivulelwa yizisebenzi izimbobo ophahleni Iwesiduli. Kodwa ngaphambi kokuba baphume omakoti laba nabakhwenyana bayogcagca kuphuma kuqala amasotsha ngobuningi bawo aqaphe. Kusemuva kokundizandiza-ke lapho indlovukaz) noma inhlwabusi yensikazi iphakamisa isinqe ikhafule iphunga elimnandi eliheha umuhlwa wenduna oseduze uyilandele. Kwehlelwa phansi emhlabathini kuhlalwe cababa. 
Zihlala phansi maqedane lezi zinhlwabusi bese zilandelana zihamba ngambili kuhamba insikazi phambili. Zithungatha indawo ezilOzithukusa kuyona ibe yikhaya elisha. 


6.2.2.4 lmisebenzi 6.2.2.4.1 Uqumbu 
Uqumbu uzalela amaqanda azoba yizisebenzi ezizokwakha umuzi zifeze neminye imisebenzi yomndeni. Njengoba kusuke kungakabibikho zisebenzi nje amaqanda okuqala akhothwa yibo abazali kanti namaqhimiza okuqala afunzwa yibo abazali ukudla okukhiqizwa yibo. Ngasemuva kuzalelwa amaqanda achanyuselwa kuphume amasotsha okuqala. Uqumbu uthi angaqala ukuzalela aqumbe. 
Uyanwebeka kwesingenzansi. Uyawazalela amaqanda afinyelela ezi-IO 000 ngelanga. Ngenkathi eseqala 10 msebenzi akabe esanyakaza. Nenkosi ayithi nyaka. Iyalala nje lapha eceleni komkayo. 
6.2.2.4.2 Inkosi 
Munye umsebenzi wayo ukuzeka indlovukazi. 6.2.2.4.3 Izisebenzi 
Izisebenzi ziqala omunye wemisebenzi yazo emikhulu wokukhotha indlovukazi, ukuyifunza, ukufunza inkosi kanye nokufunza amasotsha. Amaqanda athi angabekwa abe ecoshwa yizisebenzi ziwaqoqa ziwabeka endaweni efanele nephephile. Ukukhothwa kwendlovukazi lokhu kunomkhulu umsebenzi. 
Lo mjulukwana okhothwa yizisebenzi ugcina usabalele nesiduli souke. Iphunga lawo yilona elibophela ndawonye amalunga omndeni ngamunye. Nanxa kungakhothwana nasezinyosini liyasebenza leli phunga njengoba sichazile. 
Izisebenzi ziqoqa izicucu lOtsharii, zamaqabunga, zembewu nokunye okunjalo ziyokwakha ngakho isidleke noma isiduli sayo imihlwa. Esidlekeni (ngaphakathi esidulini) kunenganga okuyilona khaya lenkosi nendlovukazi yayo. Asizongena ekujuleni kobuciko bokwakhiwa kwesiduli. Uma sakhiwa kusetshenziswa nenhlabathi kanye nendle yayo imihlwa. Isiduli uqobo Iwaso sakhiwa ngenhlabathi ekhishwa phansi ngenkathi kwakhiwa amagumbi esidleke. Ezinye izinhlobo zemihlwa ziyazakha iziduli ezingama .20 m ukuphakama kanye nobubanzi obungama -12 m.

"From time immemorial plants have been u'sed for their imagined, or proved medicinal qualities." (Wright: I) 
(Izimila selokhu kwathi nhlo ziyasetshenziswa zisetshenziselwa okucatshangwayo nosekunobufakazi bemisebenzi yazo kukho.) " (Wright: I) (Ngisho ngeminyaka yawo 3000 BC abaseGibhithe babez!sebenzisa. Uqhubeka athi amaGriki wona akufunda kubo abaseGibhithe tikusetshenziswa kwezimila ekwelaphenL)

Amaqabunga aso amila alinganisane esiqwini segatsha ehamba ngamabili. Elokugcina iqabunga liba lodwa. Ngobukhulu amaqabunga asuka ku -3 kuya e -10 x 1,5 kuya ku -4 em. Aluhlaza ngokuzothile ngaphezulu, kanti ngaphansi aluhlaza ngokuphaphathekile kuyela ekubeni phakathi kokuba sasibhakabhaka nokubuluhlaza okotshani. 
7.2.5.3 Izimbali zomganu 
Zinobulili obehlukene. Zisaphuzi ngokombala. Ziqhakaza phakathi kuka Septhemba no Novemba. 
7.2.5.4 Izithelo 
Umganu uthela kusukela ngo Januwari kuze kube ngu Mashi. Izithelo zawo ziluhlaza njengamaqabunga aso uma zingakavuthwa, kanti uma sezivuthiwe zinemyama namanzi amaningi. 
7.2.5.5 Indawo esimila kuyo 
Siyathanda ukumila emahlanzeni nasezindaweni ezivulekile ezithi zivame utshani kodwa zibe nezihlahla ezigqagqene. 
7.2.5.6 Okunye okuphathelene Ilomgallu 
Amagxolo awo elapha izifo ezibolisa izitho. Izithelo zawo kuphiswa ngazo ingqondovu yotshwala obubizwa ngokuthi ubuganu. Kuthiwa ngisho nezilwane zasendle ezinjengezindlovu, izimfene, izinkawu nezinsimango uma zike zawadla asevundile ziwaeosha phansi, zidakwa zibhuquze.

UMashishiliz' ongayizindlovu Ziyawukudl' amaganu kwaNongoma. 
Indlovu phela ayibe isahamba ngezinselo'uma iphuthuma indawo yehlela. Akwehleki kalula ngoba nakhu uyisishwapha umthakathi wendaba lona. 
Umane ahlale phansi ngegonondo ashishilize ngalo. Akungabazeki ukuthi wayephangisa ukuyotholana phezulu nomfowabo uZibhebhu kaMaphitha. Uma kungenjalo kubhekiswe empinikazi lapho uSuthu Iwalubhekene neZigqoza noMandlakazi.

	7.5.1 	Isingeniso 
Kungaba ngubuwula isihili nlmrabanga ukuthi abautu bakithi babengenandlela zokuzivikela ekushayweni ngumphezulu bengakafiki abelungu kuleli lawokhokho. Phela zazikhona izinyanga zezulu. Kwakungafani nje nanamhlanje osuthola nenyanga eyelapha izifo zezingane ezinjengosolo nezinye isikutshela ukuthi nezulu iyakwazi uklllibethelela. Kwakungubunyanga bekhethelo ngempela llkuphatha izulu. UIwazi Iwemithi yezulu lwalusukela ekutheni abantu bakithi babeyazi imithi noma izihlahla zasendle ezazingashaywa umphezulu njengamakiolo, ombinda, omnqandane, amaminza, omvumvu nezinye eziningi okwakukhendlwa zona kueijwe abafana kumbe kuthakwe izinsizi zezulu. Nezilwane ezingashaywa yizulu njengezimfudu nezinye okwakusetshenziswa amafutha azo ekuthakeni izithoxoyi ezineminye yale mithi esibalwe ngasenhla, babezazi kahle. Lapha ngenzansi sizobheka ezimbalwa izinhlobo zezimila ezazisetshenziselwa ukubethelela ukwelelesa komphezulu.

7.6 	Imithi yokubethelela amasimu 
Sesikushilo ukuthi kwakubaluleke kakhulu ukuba impahla yomuzi (imfuyo phela) iqiniswe. Ngokunjalo namasimu ayenoehwepheshe abethwasele ukuqinisa wona kuphela. 
Ukufeza 10 msebenzi ongaka kwakudinga ulwazi olubanzi Iwamakhubalo, amafutha ezilwane nokunye kokuphebeza iziphepho nesangquma. Nakhona lapha ulwazi Iwezimila eziyizihlahla namakhambi nezilwane okuwuehithayo umbani wezulu, lwalubaluleke kakhulu. Ngamanye amazwi kwakukhethwa lokhu okungashaywa ngumphezulu. Eminye imithi ikubethelela kokubili umuzi kanye namasimu ekushayweni yizulu. Kanti eminye isetshenziselwa ukubethelela okukodwa kwalokho kuphela. Nansi eminye yayo: 
7.6.1 	Isibinda (Umbinda) 
Sesiwuehazile umbinda. Sesishilo ukuthi uyasetshenziswa ekubetheleleni ukuba izulu lingangeni ekhaya. 
Nasemasimini uyabethela. Unqanda noma uvikela ukuhlasela kweziphepho nesiehotho. Amagxolo aso okuyi wona asetshenziswa kulokhu, asuke esethakwe neminye imikhando.

Izithelo zawo zivuthwa phakathi kuka Mashi no-Aphrili. Ngobukhulu ziba ngamamililitha ayi-9. Uma sezivuthiwe ziba sikhupha ngokuthl akuphaphatheke. 
7.6.3.5 Indawo omila kuyona 
Ugebeleweni yisihlahla sehlathi. Sivame ezindaweni ezin~awa b.ese sikhula sendlala amahlamvu aso phezu kwalo iwa. Yingakho nJe kuthlwa ugebeleweni. 
7.6.3.6 Okunye okuphathelene nogebeleweni 
Naso njengalezi esesixoxe ngazo ngasenhla, asishaywa ~gumbani, ~gi.sho sesiphume saba ugabagaba phezu kwezinye. Siyahhebeza slehithe neziphepho uma liza kabi ezilimweni.

8.1 	Isingeniso 
Njengezilwane, izinyoni nokunye kwakithi kwemvelo, utshani babuballlleke kakhulu kubantu bakithi. Ingani phela kwakufllielwa izindlu, kwelukwa izitsha zokugeina nokuphatha ukudla njengezilulu, iziehumo, amaquthu, izimbenge, iziqabetho, kanye nezinye izimpahla zasendlini njengemishanelo, amaeansi, amavovo, izikhwama, izikhetho, izampontshi nokunye. 
Kuhle sikusho nokho ukuthi okunye okusatshani okusetshenziswa ekwalukeni enye yale mpahla engenhla, akubona utshani ngempela. Sisho okunjengeneema, ikhwani, ilala, ibhuma nokunye okwelukwayo njengamaeansi, izithebe, amahlllZO , izimbenge, nokunye. Obllnye utshani buyimithi obunye bungukudla kwesintu. 
Okunye okubenza utshani bubaluleke ukuba kwabo ukudla kwemfuyo. Phela utshani yibona kudla okumqoka kwemfuyo. Imfuyo ikhuluphala ibe nenyama ikhiphe nobisi oluningi uma idla yesutha. Ngaphandle kotshani akulula ukufuya, ikakhulukazi izinlComo. 
Nazi ezinye izinhlobo zotshani ezibalulekile.

8.6 	Umthente 
	8.6.1 	Ubunjalo bawo 
Utshani obudume ngegama lobu. Buneziqu ezihamba ngaphansi enhlabathini. Lezi ziqu ezinamalunga zimhloshana, kokunye zibethuma ngombala. Kuyenzeka ukhule ube ngama -120 em. Amaeembe afinyelela e -150 em ngobude kanti izihloko zawo zieijile ikakhulukazi amasha asuke esamila. Ebusika ayaguquka umbala wawo ube bomvu kokunye ube nsundu ngokubomvu. 
Impokwe yabo iqala ngokuba mhlophe bese iba namaeashazi ansomi ngokumnyama ebulilini besifazane, bese iba phuzi ngokunsundu kobesilisa. 
8.6.2 Indawo obumiJa kuyona 
Utshani bamaxhaphozi lobu. Buvamile emaxhaphozini asezindaweni ezigudla ulwandle. 
8.6.3 Ukubaluleka kwabo 
Imfuyo ayibuthandi neze lobu tshani. Buwusizo ekunqandeni ukuguguleka kwenhlabathi ezindaweni ezingamaxhaphozi. 
Kunanesaga esithi: "Umthente uhlaba usamila", esisho ukuthi umntwana uzibonakalisa esemneane ukuthi uyoba ngumuntu onjani uma esekhulile. Singakusho futhi nokuthi ikusasa lakhe umuntu kuhle alilungisele esenamandla. Lokhu kushiwo ngenxa yakho lokhu kuhlaba kwamaeembe esesikuehaze ngenhla.

1.1.4 Ukubaluleka kokufuywa kwezinyamazane kwezomnotho 
Indlela ebonakala kahle kakhulu nakalula futhi yokubaluleka kokufuywa kwezinyamazane, yinzuzo lokhu okuyilethayo njengezinto ezinokudayiseka zilethe imali masinyane: Ezinyamazaneni kungatholakala inyama enokusetshenziswa ekhaya idliwe, inyama engangenisa imali ngokuba idayiswe. Ezinyamazaneni esezibulewe kungatholakala inzuzo ngokudayisa lokhu: izikhumba, izimpondo, izinsclwa, inyama, amafutha kanye namathambo. Lokhu konke kungasetshenziswa ekwenzeni izinto ezingamagugu. 
Naru<a inyamazane efuyiwe ingadayiswa iphila kulabo abafisa ukuzidlela kanye nabafuyi abaqalayo ukufuya, izivakashi ezivela emazweni aphesheya njengoba ngikhuluma nje (1993) azikugqiziqakala ukukhokha ngaphezulu kwama-R800 ngokuzingela zibulale iNyala eyodwa zwi bese zithatha izimpondo ziyohlobisa ngazo emakubo. Akuzisolisi ngalutho futhi ukukhokha ngaphezulu kwe-R I 500 zikhokhela ukuzingela indlulamithi eyodwa. 
Umkhombe wona ziwukhokhela imali eyevile ezi-R3 000 ngaphandle kwensolo. Ngalena kokukhokhela ilungelo lokuzingela inyamazane zibuye zikhokhele namadlangala okuthukusa amakhanda esiqiwini sakho. Muningi umnotho ongenayo ovela kwamanye amazwe ufika nalezi zivakashi. 
U.5 Ukubaluleka kokufuywa kwezinyamazane kwezokuzithokozisa Ziningana izindlela zokuzithokozisa ngezilwane zasendle. Abanye abantu bavakashela epulazini (hhayi isiqiwu) lezinyamazane ukuze nje bathole ithuba lokuzibuka izinyamazane bazithathe nezithombe, lokhu bakwenza endaweni yemvelo lapho ziziphilela khona ubuhlambi kazalusile. Futhi-ke kulolu hlobo Iwesiqiwu, ovakashile ubanethuba elihle lokuzishayela nangonyawo ngaphandle kokwesaba izilwane. 
U.6 Ukubaluleka kokufuywa kwezinyamazane emfundweni Abaphokophelele ukufunda ngemveJo bathola ingqayizivele yethuba lokuzibonela ngawabo eduzane izinhlobonhlobo zezinyamazane bafunde ngazo. Kutholakala kuphephile ukuzifundela kulezi ndawo ngenxa yokungabibikho kwezilwane eziyingozi. 
1.1.7 Ukubaluleka kokufuywa kwezinyamazane ekucwaningeni 
	. . 	. 
yokuphepha okungabanga abacwaningi bazihambele nje phansi bengesabi lutho. Iningi lokucwaninga ohlangothini Iwemvelo nolokwelapha osekwake kwenziwa kusetshenziswa izilwane zasendle nokwakuzilwane zasendle. 
Kungenzeka nje ukuthi ezinye zezilwane ebezinganakekile kube yizona ezisetshenziswayo zibelusizo ekwelapheni nasekusimamiseni impilo yesintu. Asinakungabaza ukuthi ezinye zezilwane esizivumela ukuba zibhuqabhuqeke zishabalale ezweni yizona kanye ezingalekelela ekuthombululeni izinkinga zempilo yesintu uma zazingavunyelwanga zashabalala. 
Umlando wezwekazi leli lakithi ukubeka obala bha ukuthi kuleli lakithi e-Afrika kwakungenyamazane, zazigqanqula zitshakadula emagangeni, zicanasa, zingazi nanyaka. Yikho lokho okwenza zibukeke sekulubala namhlanje nxa kuqhathaniswa nasendulo.

10.2 Ukubaluleka kwezihlahla 
Abantu abaningi abangaze bangacabanga ukuthi izihlahla zibaluleke kangakanani ezilwaneni, ngenkathi bezicekela ph ansi izihlahla lezi. Kunobudlelwano obubaluleke kabi phakathi kwalokhu kokubili, yize kulukhuni ukubuqonda. 
Ake siqalc ngokubhcka iphansi lehlathi. Ayikho indawo ekwazi ukwemukela amanzi iwamumathe kangcono kunephansi lehlathi. Iphansi lchlathi lakhiwe umbola owake waba yiziqu zezihlahla, amahlamvu, inxoza, amaqabunga, izithelo, izimbali, izidumbu kanye nobulongwe bezilwane, izinyoni nezinambuzane ezazidlana zodwa zisaphila kumbe zidle izimila. 
Izimilana ezincane ezinjcngolcle okuyilona mhlandla wemvundo, izilwanyana ezinye ezincanyanyana ezingenakubonakala ngeso lenyama ezinhlobonhlobo 
zigcwele ehlathini. 
Ngaphansi kwamagxolo eziqu zczihlahla czomile, ikakhulukazi naphansi kwamaqabunga kuzithukusa izilwanc czincane zehlathi ezinjengofezcla, amashongololo, izinkume, nezinye cziningi. Ezinye izihlahla zehlathi ziwukudla 
ezilwancni zasendle nasemfuyweni. 
Okwesibili-ke masibheke ubudlelwano phakathi kwczihlahla nezinambuzane. Njengoba sesike sachaza izinyosi yizona abaqholi abakhulu ukwedlula yonke into bczitshalo zethu kanye nezihlahla zehlathi. Ezihlahleni zehlathi (zemvelo) eziqholwa yizinambuzane sizobala ezimbalwa njc, ezinjcngo: msishane, omdakane, omhlambamanzi, nezinyc eziningi. ngczinambuzane.

,ihlahla zinikeza umpheme ezinambuzaneni eziningi. lminkenke nezimbobo eziba ~mkhiwaneni, ontombikayibhinci zithukusa izinambuzane eziningi ezijika zidonse ldathane yezinyoni ezinjengamaqola nezinye eziningi. Ngisho nezincwincwi iyazidla izicabucabu futhi zisebenzise nolwembu ekwakheni izidleke zazo. 
'ukhona yini ubudlelwano phakathi kwezithelo, izinyoni nezilwane zasendle zingabancelisi abamizimba efudumele? Yebo bukhona. Izithelo yilona songo Iiphakathi kwezinyoni, izilwane nezihlahla. 
:zinye izithelo zasendle ziwukudla nakithina sintu, futhi zidliwa yizimfene, izinkawu, izindlovu, izingungumbane, izinyoni nezinambuzane. lzinyoni ikhonze izithelo ezinamanzi amaningi zibe nenyama encane. Ngakolunye hlangothi izinyoni azivamile ukudla izithelo ezinjengezomganu ngenxa yokuba -ukhuni kakhulu kwezikhumba zazo izithelo lezi. Abanye opholi, izimfene kanye ,ezintibane ziyawaqhephula amagobolondo ezithelo zidle okuphakathi. Ziningi zilwane ezikhonze lezi zithelo eziphawulwe lapha ngasenhla. Zisuka endlovini :uye kubhejane, impofu, umgankla, ingungumbane, inkawu, isinkwe, idube, ngulube yasendle, impunzi, iqhina, impala, iphiva, impalampala nomziki. 
zinyoni ezikhonze izithelo amajuba namahobhe kumbe namavukuthu, mikholwane, amakhunatha, iziqophamithi, amaphothwe nezinye eziningi. Izinyoni :zinjengezimpangele zona zithanda izithelo zezihlahla zohlobo Iwenhlokoshiyane. zimfene zona zithanda kakhulu izinhlamvu zomsasane. Imbewu yomsasane kanye leyomunga zinokudla okwaziwa ngokuthi ama 'protheni' okuningi. 
Cumele kucace kule ncazelo engasenhla ukuthi akunakwenzeka ukuba ~setshenziswe ngokweqile kumbe kulinyazwe elilodwa kula masongo-okusho Ikuthi: inhlabathi, amanzi, umoya, ukusebenza kwemisebe yelanga, izihlahla, 
10.3 Ukubaluleka kwezinyoka 
Nezinyoka zinendawo ebalulekile ensongensongeni yempilo. Iqiniso okufanele likhumbuleke ukuthi uvalo ngezinyoka luya ngokungazi ngokwanele ngazo. Siyazi ukuthi ukuzondana okukhona phakathi kwethu nezinyoka namhlanje kuthiwa selokhu kwasuka esivandeni sase-Edeni, okuxoxwa ngaso eNcwadini Eyingcwele. 
Akekho ongalibalekela iqiniso lokuthi imithonseyana yezinyoka zelakithi kuhle yesatshwe, njengoba sesikuchazile ukuziphatha kwazo. Nanxa sibheka izinto ezidliwa yizinyoka njengoba sesenzile nje, kufanele kusikhanyele ukuthi naphezu kokuba izinyoka zithathwa njengezitha zethu kodwa ngakolunye uhlangothi zingabangane bethu ngezindlela eziningi. Kuhle kuphezwe manje ukuthi isilwane silusizo kumunlU kuphela ngoba silusizo ngqo kuyena. Kufanele kwamukeleke Likuthi ngokudla amagundane ethwala izifo nezinye izilwane ezidla ziququde zibhuqabhuqe ukudla kwesinlU, zenza lukhulu zilwenzela thina sintu. 
Lezi zinyoka eziphawulwe lapha ngenhla ziphila ngokudla izinyoni, izinwabu, amaselesele, kodwa ikakhulukazi izilwane eziququdayo ezinjengamagundane namavondwe. Akulona yini usizo kithina ukuncishiswa kwezilwane esithi ziyizitha zethu na? Bheka futhi ukuthi sithe uhlobo lwenyoka ngayinye ludlani. 
Kuyathokozisa ukuthi ezinye zezinyoka zakithi ezingenangozi ngisho bengakaziwa abelungu kuleli lakithi zazivikeleka ngenxa yokuthathwa kwazo njengamadlozi. Sesizibalile-ke ezinye zazo. 
Ikhambi ekuvikelweni kwezinyoka zakithi ezingengozi, ukuba thina sikwazi ukuzahlukanisa, sazi ezinesihlungu nezingenaso njengoba kwakunjalo endulo ngezikhathi zawokhokho. Kungaba yingenxa yalolu lwazi kuphela lapho kungavikeleka khona izinyoka ezingeyona ingozi nasemakhaya ethu mbala ngoba lokho kuyosho ukuzuza kith ina luqobo ngomuso. 
10.4 Isiphetho 
Enthlabeni oqhephuka amadwala, ohhedlezela inhlabathi ihhihlika, okuvunguza kuwo umoya uphephetha, kubhananaze nenhlamvu yelanga nesango sayo, kugobhoze namanzi ageleze, kwanda nesintu ngejubane elibabazekayo, izidalwa zendalo ziphila kanje-ke. Ubuhle bemvelo yomhlaba yikhona kanye lokhu njengoba sikukhombisa kule nsongensonge yempilo.
